       printf - format and print data[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m

       [1mprintf[0m [4mOPTION[24m[m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       Print  ARGUMENT(s) according to FORMAT, or execute according to[m
       OPTION:[m
[m
       [1m--help[0m display this help and exit[m
[m
       [1m--version[0m[m
              output version information and exit[m
[m
       FORMAT controls the output as in  C  printf.   Interpreted  se‚Äê[m
       quences are:[m
[m
       \"     double quote[m
[m
       \\     backslash[m
[m
       \a     alert (BEL)[m
[m
       \b     backspace[m
[m
       \c     produce no further output[m
[m
       \e     escape[m
[m
       \f     form feed[m

[1mNAME[0m[m
       printf - format and print data[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1mprintf[0m [4mFORMAT[24m [[4mARGUMENT[24m]...[m
       [1mprintf[0m [4mOPTION[24m[m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m

       printf - format and print data[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m

       [1mprintf[0m [4mOPTION[24m[m

[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       Print  ARGUMENT(s) according to FORMAT, or execute according to[m
       OPTION:[m
[m
       [1m--help[0m display this help and exit[m
[m
       [1m--version[0m[m
              output version information and exit[m
[m
       FORMAT controls the output as in  C  printf.   Interpreted  se‚Äê[m
       quences are:[m
[m
       \"     double quote[m
[m
       \\     backslash[m
[m
       \a     alert (BEL)[m
[m
       \b     backspace[m
[m
       \c     produce no further output[m
[m
       \e     escape[m
[m
       \f     form feed[m

[?2004l[?1049h[22;0;0t[?1h=PRINTF(1)                    User Commands                   PRINTF(1)[m
[m
[1mNAME[0m[m
       printf - format and print data[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1mprintf[0m [4mFORMAT[24m [[4mARGUMENT[24m]...[m
       [1mprintf[0m [4mOPTION[24m[m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       Print  ARGUMENT(s) according to FORMAT, or execute according to[m
       OPTION:[m
[m
       [1m--help[0m display this help and exit[m
[m
       [1m--version[0m[m
              output version information and exit[m
[m
       FORMAT controls the output as in  C  printf.   Interpreted  se‚Äê[m
       quences are:[m
[m
       \"     double quote[m
[m
       \\     backslash[m
[m
       \a     alert (BEL)[m
[m
       \b     backspace[m
[m
       \c     produce no further output[m
[m
       \e     escape[m
[m
       \f     form feed[m
[7m Manual page printf(1) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K[m
[7m Manual page printf(1) line 2 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K       \n     new line[m
[7m Manual page printf(1) line 3 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K[m
[7m Manual page printf(1) line 4 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K       \r     carriage return[m

[m
[1mNAME[0m[m
       printf - format and print data[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1mprintf[0m [4mFORMAT[24m [[4mARGUMENT[24m]...[m
       [1mprintf[0m [4mOPTION[24m[m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       Print  ARGUMENT(s) according to FORMAT, or execute according to[m
       OPTION:[m
[m
       [1m--help[0m display this help and exit[m
[m
       [1m--version[0m[m
              output version information and exit[m
[m
       FORMAT controls the output as in  C  printf.   Interpreted  se‚Äê[m
       quences are:[m
[m
       \"     double quote[m
[m
       \\     backslash[m
[m
       \a     alert (BEL)[m
[m
       \b     backspace[m
[m
       \c     produce no further output[m
[m
       \e     escape[m
[m
       \f     form feed[m
[7m Manual page printf(1) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K[?1l>[?1049l[23;0;0t[?2004h10:00:27 [01;32mnik[01;34m ~[01;33m (master)[01;34m $[00m man printf--all printf[3Pa[C[C[C[C[C[C[C[3P-helpA printfcat[C[C[C[C[C[C[C[C[C[Cprintf -Aall[2Pman 3 printf

[1mNAME[0m[m
       printf - format and print data[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1mprintf[0m [4mFORMAT[24m [[4mARGUMENT[24m]...[m
       [1mprintf[0m [4mOPTION[24m[m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       Print  ARGUMENT(s) according to FORMAT, or execute according to[m
       OPTION:[m
[m
       [1m--help[0m display this help and exit[m
[m
       [1m--version[0m[m
              output version information and exit[m
[m
       FORMAT controls the output as in  C  printf.   Interpreted  se‚Äê[m
       quences are:[m
[m
       \"     double quote[m
[m
       \\     backslash[m
[m
       \a     alert (BEL)[m
[m
       \b     backspace[m
[m
       \c     produce no further output[m
[m
       \e     escape[m
[m
       \f     form feed[m

The[K[14;1Hdifferences are listed below.[16;1H   Due to shell aliases and built-in ‚Äòprintf‚Äô functions, using an[17;1Hunadorned ‚Äòprintf‚Äô interactively or in a script may get you different[18;1Hfunctionality than that described here.  Invoke it via ‚Äòenv‚Äô (i.e., ‚Äòen[18;72H\[19;1Hv[20;1Hprintf ...‚Äô) to avoid interference from the shell.[22;1H   ‚Ä¢ The FORMAT argument is reused as necessary to convert all the give[22;72H\[23;1Hn[24;1H     ARGUMENTs.  For example, the command ‚Äòprintf %s a b‚Äô outputs ‚Äòab‚Äô.[26;1H   ‚Ä¢ Missing ARGUMENTs are treated as null strings or as zeros,[27;1H     depending on whether the context expects a string or a number. [1mNAME[0m[m
       uname - print system information[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1muname[0m [[4mOPTION[24m]...[m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       Print certain system information.  With no OPTION, same as [1m-s[0m.[m
[m
       [1m-a[0m, [1m--all[0m[m
              print  all  information,  in the following order, except[m
              omit [1m-p[0m and [1m-i[0m if unknown:[m
[m
       [1m-s[0m, [1m--kernel-name[0m[m
              print the kernel name[m
[m
       [1m-n[0m, [1m--nodename[0m[m
              print the network node hostname[m
[m
       [1m-r[0m, [1m--kernel-release[0m[m
              print the kernel release[m
[m
       [1m-v[0m, [1m--kernel-version[0m[m
              print the kernel version[m
[m
       [1m-m[0m, [1m--machine[0m[m
              print the machine hardware name[m
[m
       [1m-p[0m, [1m--processor[0m[m
              print the processor type (non-portable)[m
[m
       [1m-i[0m, [1m--hardware-platform[0m[m

[1mNAME[0m[m
       uname - get name and information about current kernel[m
[m
[1mSYNOPSIS[0m[m
       [1m#include[0m [1m<sys/utsname.h>[0m[m
[m
       [1mint[0m [1muname(struct[0m [1mutsname[0m [1m*[0m[4mbuf[24m[1m);[0m[m
[m
[1mDESCRIPTION[0m[m
       [1muname[0m()  returns system information in the structure pointed to[m
       by [4mbuf[24m.  The [4mutsname[24m struct is defined in [4m<sys/utsname.h>[24m:[m
[m
           struct utsname {[m
               char sysname[];    /* Operating system name (e.g., "Linux[m ") */[m
               char nodename[];   /* Name within "some implementation-de[m fined[m
                                     network" */[m
               char release[];    /* Operating system release[m
                                     (e.g., "2.6.28") */[m
               char version[];    /* Operating system version */[m
               char machine[];    /* Hardware identifier */[m
           #ifdef _GNU_SOURCE[m
               char domainname[]; /* NIS or YP domain name */[m
           #endif[m
           };[m
[m
       The length of the arrays in a  [4mstruct[24m  [4mutsname[24m  is  unspecified[m
       (see NOTES); the fields are terminated by a null byte ('\0').[m
[m
[1mRETURN[0m [1mVALUE[0m[m
       On  success,  zero  is returned.  On error, -1 is returned, and[m
[7m Manual page uname(2) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KAA[K[K[7m Manual page uname(2) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KAA[K[K[7m Manual page uname(2) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KAA[K[K[7m Manual page uname(2) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KAA[K[K[7m Manual page uname(2) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KAA[K[K[7m Manual page uname(2) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KAA[K[K[7m Manual page uname(2) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KAA[K[K[7m Manual page uname(2) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KAA[K[K[7m Manual page uname(2) line 1 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K
